// request pbjs bids when it loads
  pbjs.que.push(function() {
    pbjs.rp.requestBids({ 
callback: callAdserver, gptSlotObjects: gpt_slot_objects.filter(function(element, index) { 
return (element) ? true : false; }) });
});

// failsafe in case PBJS doesn't load
setTimeout(function() {
callAdserver(gpt_slot_objects);
}, 2000);
});

function callAdserver(gptSlots) {
    if (pbjs.adserverCalled) return;
    pbjs.adserverCalled = true;
    googletag.pubads().refresh(gptSlots);
  }
  
   function removeElement(classname) {
   var elem = document.getElementsByClassName(classname)[0];
   return elem.parentNode.removeChild(elem);
 }
</script>

<script>
var scrollState = 'top';
$(window).scroll(function(){ 
var scrollPos = $(window).scrollTop();

    if( ( scrollPos != 100 ) && ( scrollState === 'top' ) ) {
        $(".bn_skin").stop().animate({top: '90px'}, 300);
        scrollState = 'scrolled';
    }       
    else if( ( scrollPos === 0 ) && ( scrollState === 'scrolled' ) ) {
        $(".bn_skin").stop().animate({top: '45px'}, 300);
        scrollState = 'top';
    }

});
</script>

<script lang="javascript" type="text/javascript">
    $("#toggle-temanmudik").on("click", function () {
        if (!$(this).parent(".cb-temanmudik-2026").hasClass("cb-temanmudik-2026--small")) {
            $(this).parent(".cb-temanmudik-2026").addClass("cb-temanmudik-2026--small");
            $(this).attr("dtr-evt", "giant hl teman mudik");
            $(this).attr("dtr-sec", "button hide");
            $(this).attr("dtr-act", "button hide");
            _pt(this);
        } else {
            $(this).parent(".cb-temanmudik-2026").removeClass("cb-temanmudik-2026--small");
            $(this).attr("dtr-evt", "giant hl teman mudik");
            $(this).attr("dtr-sec", "button show");
            $(this).attr("dtr-act", "button show");
            _pt(this);
        }
    });

    function toggleTemanMudik() {
        var livestreaming = ``;

        if (livestreaming != ''){
            $("#toggle-temanmudik").click();
        }
    }

    toggleTemanMudik();
</script>

<script>
 function onPrev(name) {
 const container = document.querySelector(`[data-container="${name}"]`);
 const childWidth = container.children[0].offsetWidth;
 container.scrollLeft -= childWidth;
 }
 function onNext(name) {
 const container = document.querySelector(`[data-container="${name}"]`);
 const childWidth = container.children[0].offsetWidth;
 container.scrollLeft += childWidth;
 }
 function inviewHorizontal (el, isIntersectCallback) {
 const container = document.querySelector('.itp__articleContainer');
 const items = el;
 const options = {
 root: container,
 rootMargin: '0px',
 threshold: 0.1
 };
 const callback = (entries, observer) => {
 entries.forEach((entry) => {
 if (entry.isIntersecting) {
 observer.unobserve(entry.target);
 if (isIntersectCallback) {
 isIntersectCallback(entry.target)
 }
 }
 });
 };
 const observer = new IntersectionObserver(callback, options);
 items.forEach(item => observer.observe(item));
 }
 function lazyImageHorizontal(el){
 inviewHorizontal(document.querySelectorAll(el), async function (target) {
 const item = $(target)
 const imgFlash = item.find('.itp_img-flash')
 let ratio = imgFlash.attr('data-ratio');
 let defaultImg = 'https://awscdn.detik.net.id/detik2/images/default-' + (ratio ? ratio : 11) + '.gif';
 imgFlash.on('error', function () {
 imgFlash.attr('src', defaultImg);
 });
 imgFlash.hide();
 imgFlash.closest('.lqd').css("background-image", "url(" + imgFlash.attr('data-src') + ")");
 imgFlash.attr('src', imgFlash.attr('data-src'));
 imgFlash.attr('d-loaded', 1)
 var $parent = item.find('.media__link');
 if($parent.hasClass('media__link')) {
 const videoId = $parent.attr('data-id')
 const video = FlashPilihan.videos.find(video => video.id === videoId)
 const detikBigDataSdk = await FlashPilihan.detikBigDataSdk()
 $parent.attr({
 'dtr-evt': "box flash",
 'dtr-sec': "video flash",
 'dtr-act': "video flash",
 'onclick': "_pt(this)",
 'dtr-idx': video.number,
 'dtr-id': video.id,
 'dtr-ttl': video.title
 })
 if (detikBigDataSdk) {
 detikBigDataSdk.collectEvent('show', {
 enter_from_doc_id: '',
 doc_id: videoId,
 spm: `desktop$##$detikcom$##$boxflash$##$${video.number}`
 });
 }
 }
 })
 }

 const videosIdTahan = this.videos.map(function (video) {
 return video.id
 })
 if (! excludeStrVideosId) {
 return videosIdTahan

 return excludeVideosId.concat(videosIdTahan)

 'https://recg20.detik.com/article-recommendation',
 'https://rech20.detik.com/article-recommendation'
 ]
 const baseUrlRec = baseUrlRecs[this.randomIndex]
 return `${baseUrlRec}/wp/${this.cookieDtma}`
 },

 return '-'
 }

 async request () {
 return await fetch(this.url, {
 method: 'POST',
 headers: {
 'Content-Type': 'application/json'
 },
 body: JSON.stringify({
 size: this.size,
 excludeProgramIds: this.excludeProgramIds,
 excludeDocs: this.excludeDocs,
 isVertical: true
 })
 })
 },
 async getData () {
 const req = await this.request()
 const data = await req.json()
 let indexArticle = 0
 let dataPilihan = [];
 
 this.videos.forEach((video) => {
 dataPilihan.push({
 duration: video.duration,
 imageurl: video.image,
 videourl: `https://20.detik.com${video.slug_20detik}`,
 number: indexArticle,
 id: video.id,
 title: video.title,
 animated: video.animated
 })
 })
 let allData = [];
 const dataRecs = data.body;
 allData = dataPilihan.concat(dataRecs)
 this.videos = allData
 let articlesHtml = allData.map((row, i) => {
 indexArticle += 1
 row.number = indexArticle
 return this.articleTemplate(row)
 }).join('')
 articlesHtml += `
 <article class="slider-snap__item slider-snap__item--index">
 <div class="media media--image-radius block-link">
 <div class="media__image mg-0">
 <span class="ratiobox ratiobox--9-16"></span>

 </div>

 <i class="icon icon--sm icon-chevron-right mx-auto mgb-16"></i>
 Lihat Lebih Banyak
 </a>
 </div>
 </article>`
 $('.itp__articleContainer').prepend(articlesHtml)
 helper.lqd_img('.lqd')
 },
 detikBigDataSdk () {
 if (typeof detikBigDataSdk !== 'undefined') {
 return Promise.resolve(detikBigDataSdk)
 }
 if (typeof detikBigDataSdk === 'undefined') {
 return new Promise((resolve) => {
 const checkInterval = 100
 let waitedTime = 0
 const intervalId = setInterval(() => {
 waitedTime += checkInterval
 if (typeof detikBigDataSdk !== 'undefined' || waitedTime >= 3000) {
 clearInterval(intervalId)
 resolve(detikBigDataSdk)
 }
 }, checkInterval)
 })
 }
 return Promise.resolve()
 },
 async init () {
 this.randomIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * this.srcModels.length)
 const observer = new IntersectionObserver(function (entries) {
 entries.forEach(async function (entry) {
 if (entry.isIntersecting) {
 await FlashPilihan.getData()
 lazyImageHorizontal('.itp__boxFlashItem');
 observer.disconnect()
 }
 })
 }, {
 rootMargin: "0px 0px 300px 0px"
 });
 observer.observe(document.querySelector('.itp__articleContainer'))
 }
 }
 $(function () {
 FlashPilihan.init()
 })
</script><!--cached @ 1774262314--><!--replaced-->            <!-- S:promobox --><div style="margin:10px 1px 10px 0 ; text-align:center">

<!-- SCRIPT REFRESH SLOT MR1 SAAT VIEWPORT -->
<script>
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
    var adSlot_mr1 = document.getElementById('div-gpt-ad-1572110512991-0');

    // Jika elemen tidak ditemukan, buat div MR1
    if (!adSlot_mr1) {
        adSlot_mr1 = document.createElement('div');
        adSlot_mr1.id = 'div-gpt-ad-1572110512991-0';
        adSlot_mr1.style.width = '300px';
        adSlot_mr1.style.height = '600px';
        document.body.insertBefore(adSlot_mr1, document.body.firstChild);
    }

    var refreshInterval_mr1 = null; // Interval refresh
    var visibilityStartTime = null; // Waktu awal iklan terlihat
    var visibilityTimeout = null;
    var isTabActive = true; // Cek apakah tab aktif

    function refreshAd_mr1() {
        console.log('🔄 Memanggil fungsi refreshAd_mr1()...');
        if (typeof gpt_mr1 !== 'undefined' && isTabActive) {
            googletag.cmd.push(function () {
                console.log('✅ MR1 sedang di-refresh...');
                googletag.pubads().refresh([gpt_mr1]);
                console.log('✅ MR1 refreshed at ' + new Date().toLocaleTimeString());
            });
        } else {
            console.log('⚠️ gpt_mr1 tidak terdefinisi atau tab tidak aktif!');
        }
    }

    var observer_mr1 = new IntersectionObserver(function (entries) {
        entries.forEach(function (entry) {
            if (entry.intersectionRatio >= 0.7) { // Visibility 70%+
                console.log("👀 MR1 terlihat lebih dari 70%, mulai hitung waktu...");

                if (!visibilityStartTime) {
                    visibilityStartTime = new Date().getTime();

                    visibilityTimeout = setTimeout(function () {
                        let now = new Date().getTime();
                        if (now - visibilityStartTime >= 3000) { // Delay 3 detik
                            if (!refreshInterval_mr1) {
                                refreshInterval_mr1 = setInterval(refreshAd_mr1, 35000); // Refresh tiap 35 detik
                                console.log("🔄 MR1 refresh akan berjalan setiap 35 detik.");
                            }
                        }
                    }, 5000);
                }
            } else {
                console.log("🚫 MR1 tidak terlihat minimal 70%, reset waktu & hentikan refresh.");

                visibilityStartTime = null;
                clearTimeout(visibilityTimeout);

                if (refreshInterval_mr1) {
                    clearInterval(refreshInterval_mr1);
                    refreshInterval_mr1 = null;
                    console.log("⏹️ MR1 refresh dihentikan.");
                }
            }
        });
    }, { threshold: 0.7 }); // Aktif jika 70% iklan terlihat

    // Cek apakah user berpindah tab atau kembali
    document.addEventListener("visibilitychange", function () {
        isTabActive = !document.hidden;
        if (!isTabActive) {
            console.log("⏸️ Tab tidak aktif, hentikan refresh.");
            clearInterval(refreshInterval_mr1);
            refreshInterval_mr1 = null;
        } else {
            console.log("▶️ Tab kembali aktif, lanjutkan refresh jika MR1 masih terlihat.");
        }
    });

    if (adSlot_mr1) {
        observer_mr1.observe(adSlot_mr1);
        googletag.cmd.push(function () { googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-1572110512991-0'); });
    }
});
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
$(function() {
    // Custom Searchable Dropdown
    $(document).on('click', '.prayer-times__select-trigger', function(e) {
        var wrapper = $(this).closest('.prayer-times__select-wrapper');
        $('.prayer-times__select-wrapper').not(wrapper).removeClass('open');
        wrapper.toggleClass('open');
        if (wrapper.hasClass('open')) {
            wrapper.find('.prayer-times__select-input').focus();
        }
        e.stopPropagation();
    });

    $(document).on('input', '.prayer-times__select-input', function() {
        var val = $(this).val().toLowerCase();
        var options = $(this).closest('.prayer-times__select-dropdown').find('.prayer-times__select-option');
        options.each(function() {
            var text = $(this).text().toLowerCase();
            $(this).toggle(text.indexOf(val) > -1);
        });
    });

    $(document).on('click', '.prayer-times__select-option', function() {
        var val = $(this).data('value');
        var text = $(this).text();
        var wrapper = $(this).closest('.prayer-times__select-wrapper');
        var displayText = text;
        if (displayText.length > 11) {
            displayText = displayText.substring(0, 11) + '...';
        }
        wrapper.find('.prayer-times__select-trigger').text(displayText);
        wrapper.find('.prayer-times__select-option').removeClass('selected');
        $(this).addClass('selected');
        wrapper.removeClass('open');
        // You can add logic here to trigger actual prayer time update
        
        $(this).attr('dtr-evt', 'giant hl ramadan');
        $(this).attr('dtr-sec', 'lokasi adzan');
        $(this).attr('dtr-act', 'lokasi adzan');
        $(this).attr('dtr-ttl', text);

        _pt(this);
        
		document.cookie = `_city=${val}; path=/; domain=.detik.com; max-age=${30 * 24 * 60 * 60}`;

        window.open('https://www.detik.com/hikmah/ramadan/jadwal-sholat?page='+ val, '_blank');

        console.log('Selected city:', val);
    });

    $(document).on('click', function() {
        $('.prayer-times__select-wrapper').removeClass('open');
    });

    $(document).on('click', '.prayer-times__select-dropdown', function(e) {
        e.stopPropagation();
    });

    $('.prayer-times__select-trigger').each(function() {
        var text = $(this).text();
        if (text.length > 9) {
            $(this).text(text.substring(0, 9) + '...');
        }
    });
})
</script>
<script type="text/javascript" src="https://awscdn.detik.net.id/assets/js/jadwal-sholat.js?v=202603231775"></script>

<script lang="javascript" type="text/javascript">
    function setTanggalRamadan(){
        var startRamadhan = new Date('');
        var jumlahHari = 0;
        var today = new Date();

        startRamadhan.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
        today.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);

        if (today >= startRamadhan) {
            var selisihHari = Math.floor((today - startRamadhan) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24)) + 1;

            if (selisihHari <= jumlahHari) {
                $("#date_hijriah").text(selisihHari + " RAMADAN 1447 H");
            }
        }
    }

    setTanggalRamadan();

    $(document).ready(function () {
        var url = 'wss://push.detik.com/ws/popoutnotif';
        helper.ws(url, function (data) {
            if(data) {
                var d = JSON.parse(data)
                if(d.type == 'kultum'){
                    if (d.status == 'on' || d.status == 'off') {
                        setTimeout(function(){
                            location.reload(false);
                        }, 10000);
                    }
                }
            }
        });
    });
</script>

 "https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/swiper@12/swiper-bundle.min.mjs"
 );

<script>
$(function(){
    const listArticle = document.querySelector(".adsmartside-article");
    const ArtikelShow = 6;

    const hideExtraArticles = () => {
        const articles = listArticle.querySelectorAll("article");
        articles.forEach((article, index) => {
        article.style.display = index < ArtikelShow ? "block" : "none";
        });
    };

    // Initial execution
    hideExtraArticles();

    // Watch for added articles
    const observer = new MutationObserver(() => {
        hideExtraArticles();
    });

    observer.observe(listArticle, { childList: true, subtree: true });
});
</script></div>

<script>
var loadScriptAsync = function(uri){
  return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
    var tag = document.createElement('script');
    tag.src = uri;
    tag.async = true;
    tag.onload = () => {
      resolve();
    };
  var firstScriptTag = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];
  firstScriptTag.parentNode.insertBefore(tag, firstScriptTag);
});
}
var scriptLoaded = loadScriptAsync('https://newrevive.detik.com/delivery/asyncjs.php');

scriptLoaded.then(function(){
// channelbox year in review
    //document.getElementById("rv_cb_g20").setAttribute("data-revive-zoneid", rv_cb_g20);

 window.reviveAsync["0cceecb9cae9f51a31123c541910d59b"].addEventListener('afterRenderBanner',rvCallbackBanner);

 function rvCallbackBanner(data){

  for(i=0;i<data.detail.length;i++){
  }

 }
});

function checkBannerAvailable(dataDetail, checkZone, callFunc, available = false){
	try {
		var show = available ? 1 : 0;
		if(show == 0){
          if (dataDetail.zoneid == checkZone && dataDetail.bannerid == show) {
            callFunc();
            console.log('zone id adjustment : ' + checkZone);
          }
        }
        if(show == 1){
          if (dataDetail.zoneid == checkZone && dataDetail.bannerid >= show) {
            callFunc();
            console.log('zone id adjustment : ' + checkZone);
          }
        }
	} catch(e) {
		console.log(e);
	}
}

</script>
